    ⮑ #!/bin/sh
      # Build QLever's find_package() dependencies with the Cosmopolitan toolchain
      # into a sysroot prefix ($COSMOS, default ~/cosmos). Idempotent: each dep
      # leaves a .built-<name> marker in the prefix and is skipped on re-runs.
      #
      # Versions are pinned to match conanfile.txt at the pinned QLever commit
      # (boost 1.83.0, icu 76.1, openssl 3.1.1, zstd 1.5.5) + zlib 1.3.1 for
      # Boost.Iostreams' gzip filter.
      #
      # jemalloc is intentionally NOT built: it is optional in QLever's CMake and
      # cosmo's own malloc is used instead (swap-in is a later optimization).
      set -eu
      
      COSMOCC="${COSMOCC:-$HOME/cosmocc}"
      COSMOS="${COSMOS:-$HOME/cosmos}"
      JOBS="${JOBS:-$(sysctl -n hw.ncpu 2>/dev/null || nproc)}"
      SRCDIR="$COSMOS/src"
      LOGDIR="$COSMOS/log"
      
      mkdir -p "$COSMOS" "$SRCDIR" "$LOGDIR" "$COSMOS/lib/pkgconf
            …[+2570 chars]

CLAUDE:
The glob component-matching hack I just wrote is convoluted — rewriting it cleanly:

  → Edit(replace_all=false  file_path=/home/seb/Chimera.APE/src/walk.cpp  old_string=// Glob with '*' (any run, not crossing '/'), '**' (any run incl '/'), '?'.
bool glob_match(const std::string& pattern, const std::string& path) {
  // Recursive two-pointer match; patterns are short, paths are short.
  std::function<bool(size_t, size_t)> m = [&](size_t pi, size_t si) -> bool {
    while (pi < pattern.size()) {
      char pc = pattern[pi];
      if (pc == '*') {
        bool dbl = pi + 1 < pattern.size() && pattern[pi + 1] == '*';
        size_t next = pi + (dbl ? 2 : 1);
        for (size_t k = si; k <= path.size(); ++k) {
          if (m(next, k)) return true;
          if (k < path.size() && !dbl && path[k] == '/') return false;
        }
        return false;
      }
      if (si >= path.size()) return false;
      if (pc != '?' && pc != path[si]) return false;
      ++pi, ++si;
    }
    return si == path.size();
  };
  // A bare name pattern (no '/') matches against any path component.
  if (pattern.find('/') == std::string::npos) {
    size_t start = 0;
    while (true) {
      size_t end = path.find('/', start);
      std::string comp = path.substr(start, end == std::string::npos ? end : end - start);
      std::function<bool(size_t, size_t)> dummy;  // sil

// Recursive two-pointer matcher: '*' = any run not crossing '/', '**' = any

bool glob_core(const std::string& pat, size_t pi, const std::string& s, size_t si) {
  while (pi < pat.size()) {
    char pc = pat[pi];
    if (pc == '*') {
      bool dbl = pi + 1 < pat.size() && pat[pi + 1] == '*';
      size_t next = pi + (dbl ? 2 : 1);
      for (size_t k = si; k <= s.size(); ++k) {
        if (glob_core(pat, next, s, k)) return true;
        if (k < s.size() && !dbl && s[k] == '/') return false;
      }
      return false;
    }
    if (si >= s.size()) return false;
    if (pc != '?' && pc != s[si]) return false;
    ++pi, ++si;
  }
  return si == s.size();
}
}  // namespace

bool glob_match(const std::string& pattern, const std::string& path) {
  if (glob_core(pattern, 0, path, 0)) return true;
  // A bare-name pattern (no '/') also matches any single path component,
  // mirroring gitignore: "*.log" ignores logs at every depth.
  if (pattern.find('/') == std::string::npos) {
    size_t start = 0;
    while (start <= path.size()) {
      size_t end = path.find('/', start);
      size_t len = (end == std::
      …[+210 chars])

The keyword retriever works end-to-end — chunk IRIs ranked by BM25. Recording the verified query shape in the decisions doc, then building the orchestrator with cosmocc:

  → Edit(replace_all=false  file_path=/home/seb/Chimera.APE/docs/DECISIONS.md  old_string=**Decision.** Initial ingest emits Turtle batches to a staging file and runs  new_string=**Verified text-query shape** (tested against the built APE, 2026-06-13 —
`ql:` is a *built-in* prefix for
`http://qlever.cs.uni-freiburg.de/builtin-functions/`; declaring the old
`<QLever-internal-function/>` form silently matches nothing). In
from-literals mode `ql:contains-entity` binds the literal itself, so the
keyword retriever (§6 step 3) is:

```sparql
PREFIX ch: <chimera://ontology#>
SELECT ?chunk ?ql_score_t_var_text WHERE {
  ?t ql:contains-word "term1 term2*" .
  ?t ql:contains-entity ?text .
  ?chunk ch:text ?text .
} ORDER BY DESC(?ql_score_t_var_text)
```

  → Edit(replace_all=false  file_path=/home/seb/Chimera.APE/src/supervisor.cpp  old_string=bool Child::running() const {
  if (pid_ <= 0) return false;
  return ::kill(pid_, 0) == 0;
}  new_string=bool Child::running() const {
  if (pid_ <= 0) return false;
  // Reap if exited: kill(pid, 0) alone reports zombies as alive.
  int status = 0;
  pid_t r = ::waitpid(pid_, &status, WNOHANG);
  if (r == pid_) {
    const_cast<Child*>(this)->pid_ = -1;
    return false;
  }
  return r == 0;
})

// APE binaries are valid ZIP archives; cosmocc exposes embedded assets under
// the virtual /zip/ path (§1: payloads ride inside the binary). First run
// extracts them into db/runtime/, version-stamped via a marker file, so
// children can be exec'd (you cannot exec /zip/... directly).
void extract_zip_payloads(const std::string& db_dir) {
  const char* kVersion = "v0.1.0";  // bump to re-extract on upgrade
  std::string bin = db_dir + "/runtime/bin";
  std::string stamp = bin + "/.extracted-" + kVersion;
  if (fs::exists(stamp)) return;
  if (!fs::exists("/zip/organs")) return;  // dev build: nothing embedded
  fs::create_directories(bin);
  for (const auto& f : fs::directory_iterator("/zip/organs")) {
    std::string dst = bin + "/" + f.path().filename().string();
    std::ifstream in(f.path(), std::ios::binary);
    std::ofstream out(dst, std::ios::binary | std::ios::trunc);
    out << in.rdbuf();
    out.close();
    fs::permissions(dst, fs::perms::owner_all | fs::perms::group_read |
                             fs::perms::others_read);
  }
  std::ofstream(stamp) << kVersion;
}

}  // namespace

    ⮑ ## Results
      
      ### Embeddings cluster by modality, not content
      
      Cosine similarities (mean-pooled, L2-normalized):
      
      | pair type | range |
      |---|---|
      | same modality, different topics — text | 0.85 – 0.94 |
      | same modality, different topics — image | 0.74 – 0.79 |
      | same modality, different topics — audio | 0.55 – 0.66 |
      | **same sentence, different modality** | **0.30 – 0.61** |
      
      The image embedding of the fox pangram is closer to the *pasta* text
      than to its own text. Raw cross-modal retrieval (nearest text for each
      media item): **2/6**, chance-level.

  s.bind(1, c.chunk_id).bind(2, c.doc_id).bind(3, static_cast<int64_t>(c.ordinal));

  s.bind(5, c.byte_start).bind(6, c.byte_end);
  s.exec();
}  new_string=void Manifest::insert_chunk(const ChunkRow& c) {
  Stmt s(db_,
         "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO chunk(chunkid,docid,ordinal,veckey,byte_start,byte_end,modality) "
         "VALUES(?1,?2,?3,?4,?5,?6,?7)");
  s.bind(1, c.chunk_id).bind(2, c.doc_id).bind(3, static_cast<int64_t>(c.ordinal));
  s.bind_u64(4, c.vec_key);
  s.bind(5, c.byte_start).bind(6, c.byte_end).bind(7, c.modality);
  s.exec();
}

std::vector<uint64_t> Manifest::vec_keys_of_modality(const std::string& modality) {
  Stmt s(db_, "SELECT veckey FROM chunk WHERE modality=?1");
  s.bind(1, modality);
  std::vector<uint64_t> out;
  while (s.row()) out.push_back(static_cast<uint64_t>(s.col_i64(0)));
  return out;
})

  → Edit(replace_all=false  file_path=/home/seb/Chimera.APE/src/walk.cpp  old_string=std::string mime_of(const std::string& path) {
  auto it = kMime.find(ext_of(path));
  return it != kMime.end() ? it->second : "text/plain";
}  new_string=std::string mime_of(const std::string& path) {
  std::string e = ext_of(path);
  // Media handled natively by the model (Gemma 4 multimodal pipeline).
  if (e == "png") return "image/png";
  if (e == "jpg" || e == "jpeg") return "image/jpeg";
  if (e == "wav") return "audio/wav";
  if (e == "mp3") return "audio/mpeg";
  auto it = kMime.find(e);
  return it != kMime.end() ? it->second : "text/plain";
}

std::string modality_of(const std::string& path) {
  std::string e = ext_of(path);
  if (e == "png" || e == "jpg" || e == "jpeg") return "image";
  if (e == "wav" || e == "mp3") return "audio";
  return "text";
})

  → Edit(replace_all=false  file_path=/home/seb/Chimera.APE/src/util.h  old_string=inline std::string chunk_id(const std::string& doc_id, int ordinal) {  new_string=inline std::string base64_encode(const std::string& in) {
  static const char* k =
      "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";
  std::string out;
  out.reserve((in.size() + 2) / 3 * 4);
  size_t i = 0;
  while (i + 2 < in.size()) {
    uint32_t v = (uint8_t(in[i]) << 16) | (uint8_t(in[i + 1]) << 8) | uint8_t(in[i + 2]);
    out.push_back(k[v >> 18]);
    out.push_back(k[(v >> 12) & 63]);
    out.push_back(k[(v >> 6) & 63]);
    out.push_back(k[v & 63]);
    i += 3;
  }
  if (i + 1 == in.size()) {
    uint32_t v = uint8_t(in[i]) << 16;
    out.push_back(k[v >> 18]);
    out.push_back(k[(v >> 12) & 63]);
    out += "==";
  } else if (i + 2 == in.size()) {
    uint32_t v = (uint8_t(in[i]) << 16) | (uint8_t(in[i + 1]) << 8);
    out.push_back(k[v >> 18]);
    out.push_back(k[(v >> 12) & 63]);
    out.push_back(k[(v >> 6) & 63]);
    out += "=";
  }
  return out;
}

  bool any = false;
  for (const char* name : kOrgans) any = any || fs::exists(std::string("/zip/") + name);
  if (!any) return;  // dev build: nothing embedded
  fs::create_directories(bin);
  for (const char* name : kOrgans) {
    std::string src = std::string("/zip/") + name;
    if (!fs::exists(src)) continue;
    std::string dst = bin + "/" + name;
    std::ifstream in(src, std::ios::binary);
    std::ofstream out(dst, std::ios::binary | std::ios::trunc);
    out << in.rdbuf();
    out.close();
    fs::permissions(dst, fs::perms::owner_all | fs::perms::group_read |
                             fs::perms::others_read);
  })

      Shell cwd was reset to /home/seb/Chimera.APE

CLAUDE:
Found it. `run-4191758.ttl` (k2's) has all 3 chunks (4958 bytes), but `_bulk.ttl` is 88 bytes — just the prologue. The concatenation dropped k2's real content.

The cause is a classic C++ stream gotcha: `out << in.rdbuf()` **sets failbit when the source is empty**. The killed k1 left a 0-byte `run-4191262.ttl`, which sorts first in directory order; streaming it poisons `out` with failbit, so the very next file — k2's real triples — is silently not written. The index then builds from an empty graph and reports "ok". This is precisely the kill-9 path. Fixing the concat to be robust:

  → Edit(replace_all=false  file_path=/home/seb/Chimera.APE/src/ingest.cpp  old_string=    std::string all = db_dir + "/staging/_bulk.ttl";
    {
      std::ofstream out(all, std::ios::trunc);
      out << ttl_prologue();
      for (const auto& f : fs::directory_iterator(db_dir + "/staging"))
        if (f.path().extension() == ".ttl" && f.path().filename() != "_bulk.ttl") {
          std::ifstream in(f.path());
          out << in.rdbuf();
        }
    }  new_string=    std::string all = db_dir + "/staging/_bulk.ttl";
    {
      std::ofstream out(all, std::ios::trunc);
      out << ttl_prologue();
      for (const auto& f : fs::directory_iterator(db_dir + "/staging"))
        if (f.is_regular_file() && f.path().extension() == ".ttl" &&
            f.path().filename() != "_bulk.ttl") {
          // NB: `out << in.rdbuf()` sets failbit on an EMPTY source, which
          // then silently drops every later file — and a kill -9 leaves an
          // empty run-<pid>.ttl that sorts first. Read explicitly instead.
          std::ifstream in(f.path(), std::ios::binary);
          std::string content((std::istreambuf_iterator<char>(in)), {});
          out << content;
        }
    })
    ⮑ The file /home/seb/Chimera.APE/src/ingest.cpp has been updated successfully. (file state is current in your context — no need to Read it back)

CLAUDE:
I should also add the `ch:Chunk` count to the test's check and guard against silently building an empty index. Let me add a sanity guard so this class of bug fails loudly rather than reporting "ok":

  → Edit(replace_all=false  file_path=/home/seb/Chimera.APE/src/ingest.cpp  old_string=    std::string err;
    if (!organs.build_qlever_index(all, &err)) {
      std::fprintf(stderr, "chimera: graph index build failed: %s\n", err.c_str());
    } else {
      graph_ok = true;
    }  new_string=    // Guard against building from a Turtle file that lost its triples (e.g.
    // the empty-source failbit bug above): if we wrote n_chunks chunks this
    // run, the bulk file must contain at least that many chunk triples.
    std::string err;
    int64_t ttl_chunks = 0;
    {
      std::ifstream in(all);
      std::string line;
      while (std::getline(in, line))
        if (line.find("a ch:Chunk ") != std::string::npos) ++ttl_chunks;
    }
    if (n_chunks > 0 && ttl_chunks < n_chunks) {
      std::fprintf(stderr,
                   "chimera: staged graph has %lld chunk triples but %lld were "
                   "written this run — refusing to build a truncated index\n",
                   static_cast<long long>(ttl_chunks), static_cast<long long>(n_chunks));
    } else if (!organs.build_qlever_index(all, &err)) {
      std::fprintf(stderr, "chimera: graph index build failed: %s\n", err.c_str());
    } else {
      graph_ok = true;

## What got built

Starting from `prompt.md` and your three forked organ repos, I built the whole system: a single Actually Portable Executable that fuses a llamafile (Gemma 4 12B), QLever, and TurboVec into one offline hybrid graph-vector knowledge engine. It's working end-to-end on this box.

**The spine (§2).** Triple-tap sampled identity hashing (xxh3, with `--paranoid` BLAKE3 fallback), a SQLite manifest with per-document stage watermarks, a `.chimeraignore` walker with binary sniffing, a structure-aware chunker with tiling byte-offsets and overlap, and a Turtle emitter for the §4 ontology. All covered by an assert-based test suite that's green under both native gcc and cosmocc.

**The organs.** I built all three for Cosmopolitan: the QLever APEs (`qlever-index`/`qlever-server`) and the llamafile from your forks, and — since TurboVec shipped as a library only — I wrote `turbovec-server` from scratch: a tiny Rust HTTP server over `IdMapIndex` that builds as a **fat x86_64+aarch64 APE** (via custom cosmo target specs), with a 14-check smoke suite.

**Both pipelines.** Ingest (§5): walk → identity/dedup/supersession → chunk → embed → extract (Appendix A schema, retry-once) → vector upsert → Turtle → QLever bulk-build or SPARQL UPDATE. Search (§6): ANN + BM25 → RRF → graph crawl (siblings, co-mentions with the stop-entity rule, relation receipts) → context budget → synthesis → **per-citation re-checksum verification** (`✓ verified` / `⚠ drifted` / `⚠ missing`). Plus `status`/`verify`/`vacuum`/`sparql`.

**Multimodality (your mid-build directive).** Images and audio are first-class: the model transcribes-or-describes each, that derived text flows through the normal text pipeline, and the raw media vector is stored for same-modality search. `--search-file scene.png` correctly found the image by example and answered with verified citations. I respected the modality-gap finding from your docs (text bridge is primary; media ANN is allowlist-partitioned by modality).

## Verification

The §11 acceptance suite scores **13/15**, with all real criteria passing: APE format + static, idempotent re-run (<2s/1000 docs), middle-edit supersession, `--paranoid` catching sampled-hash blind spots, verified-citation + deleted→missing, vacuum shrinking stores, and **kill-9 resume with zero duplicates**. The two non-passes: 5a is a test-design artifact (the script edits a file before searching, so the honest answer *is* `⚠ drifted`); the other was the genuine bug below.

## The bug I chased down

The kill-9 resume test (criterion 7) left the graph empty while the manifest had rows. Root cause from preserved logs: `out << in.rdbuf()` **sets failbit on an empty source file**, and a killed run leaves a 0-byte `run-<pid>.ttl` that sorts first in directory order — poisoning the stream so the resuming run's real triples were silently dropped, and QLever then built an empty index but reported "ok". Fixed by reading each staged file explicitly, plus a guard that refuses to build a truncated index. Re-verified: resume now produces a graph matching the manifest (3 chunks, 28 text-index words).

## Process notes

Everything is on `main` (with a `multimodal` branch merged in), pushed continuously as you asked. Design decisions and the gotchas I hit (cosmocc `chmod`, QLever's built-in `ql:` prefix, the rayon busy-spin, `--mmproj`, Gemma's `reasoning_content` salvage) are documented in `docs/DECISIONS.md`. The release ships `chimera.ape` (313 MB, organs embedded, weights sidecar) with full usage instructions in the notes and `docs/USAGE.md`.

One honest caveat for the alpha, as labeled in the release: ingest is sequential and CPU-bound here (~7 tok/s — minutes per document), which is why I kept the test corpora tiny per your guidance; the bounded-queue concurrency from §5 is designed but not yet wired, and it's built for the GPU you're heading toward.

## https://huggingface.co/SEBK4C/Chimera.APE

The repo is public and holds exactly what you asked for — **one download, all internals working**:

| File | Size | What it is |
|---|---|---|
| `chimera-full.ape` | 6.97 GiB (7.48 GB) | the single self-contained executable |
| `README.md` | — | model card with quick-start + multimodal usage |

The single file carries, in its APE zip store, the orchestrator plus all four organ binaries (llamafile, qlever-server, qlever-index, turbovec-server), the **Gemma 4 12B QAT q4_0 weights**, and the **multimodal projector**. I verified before publishing that it runs from a cold start with no `--model` flag and no env vars: it self-extracts everything into `.chimera/runtime/` on first run and ingests successfully (embedding dim 3840, graph ok).

A user's entire flow is now:

```sh
hf download SEBK4C/Chimera.APE chimera-full.ape --local-dir .
chmod +x chimera-full.ape
./chimera-full.ape ingest ~/notes
./chimera-full.ape --search "…" --db ~/notes/.chimera
```

No weights to fetch separately, no sidecars, no runtime deps.

**Both distribution flavors now exist**, as the spec recommended:
- **HuggingFace** — `chimera-full.ape` (7.5 GB, weights embedded) — the true single file.
- **GitHub** — [`v0.1.0-alpha`](https://github.com/SEBK4C/Chimera.APE/releases/tag/v0.1.0-alpha) — `chimera.ape` (315 MB, organs embedded, weights sidecar) for people who'd rather not pull 7.5 GB.

That completes the build end to end: spine, three organs (including the from-scratch `turbovec.ape`), both pipelines, multimodality, the kill-9 resume fix, the GitHub alpha, and now the single-file HuggingFace release.

import json
f='/home/seb/.claude/projects/-home-seb-Chimera-APE/0058f50c-9e44-4fe6-94f2-0933ebf9f7d9.jsonl'
n=0
types={}
for line in open(f):
    line=line.strip()
    if not line: continue
    try: d=json.loads(line)
    except: continue
    n+=1
    t=d.get('type','?')
    types[t]=types.get(t,0)+1
    if n<=3:
        print('--- record', n, 'keys:', list(d.keys()))
        print('  type:', t, '| role:', (d.get('message',{}) or {}).get('role'))
print('total records:', n)
print('types:', types)

    if d.get('type') not in ('user','assistant'): continue
